 congress ne buree tarah parajeet hone se pehle 516 karod rupee kharch kiye
 National parties have given details of their election expenses to the Election Commission after a lot of controversy
 chunaav ayog ke data ke mutabik, aam chunaav 2014 ke saath andhra pradesh, arunachal pradesh, odisha or sikkim vidhansabha chunaavon main ensipi ne 51 karod or bispi ne 30 karod se zyada rupye kharch kiye
 The Bharatiya Janata Party spent a total of Rs 7,14,28,57,813 while the Congress spent Rs 5,16,02,36,785
 donon partiyon ne haal hi main kharch se judi jaankareechunaav ayogko saunpi he

 vahiin congress ne pichley saal 22 disambar ko kharch se judi jaankaree chunaav ayog ko saunpi thi

 chunaav ayog ke data ke mutabik ensipi ne kul 51,34,44,854 rupye kharch kiye
 Bahujan Samaj Party's total expenditure was Rs 30,05,84,822
 sipiai(em) ne in chunaavon main 18,69,18,169 rupye kharch kiye
 The information related to CPI expenditure was given only in September 2014 last year
 iske baavjood chunaav ayog ne sipiai ke kharch kii rakam nahin bataai he
 On November 28, the Election Commission issued a show cause notice to 20 parties for not providing details of the expenditure
 isamen bijepi, congress ke saath aam aadmi party bhi shaamil thi
 The Election Commission had warned these parties that recognition could be withdrawn if they did not submit information related to the expenditure in the next 15 days

 jharkhand lok seva ayog (jepiessi) kii parikshaon main vyapak bhrashtachar ke aaropon kaa saamana kar rahi ayog kii purv sachiv elice ushaa rani singh nehzaribagh jile main apane ghar kii kurki ke turant baad police ke samaksh aatmasamarpan kar diya
 Police sources said here that former JPSC secretary Alice Usha Rani Singh surrendered before the police on Tuesday evening at Mufassil police station of Hazaribagh district, a hundred and a hundred kilometers from here
 unke aatmasamarpan ke turant baad police ne isaki soochna satarkta vibhaag ko di jiske dal ne thane pahunch kar unhen giraftaar kar liya or ranchi ravaanaa ho gayi 
 This is the first major arrest in this big scam
 singh ko aaj ranchi main vishesh satarkta adaalat main pesh kiya jaayegaa
 The Vigilance Department had been looking for him and other senior officials since registering an FIR in the matter but all senior officials including the then Secretary of the Commission Usha Rani Singh were absconding
 isse purv aaj din main vishesh satarkta adaalat ke nirdeshon evam warrant ke baavjood adaalat main upasthit nahin ho saki ushaa rani singh ke ghar kii satarkta vibhaag ne kurki kii
 The court declared him an absconder and ordered attachment of his house
 is aadesh ke aadhaar par mangalvaar ko ranchi se hazaribagh pahunche satarkta dal ne unke ghar kii kurki kii
 Police sources said that the vigilance team conducted a raid under the leadership of Deputy Superintendent Shivchand Chaubey
 mukhyamantri arjuna munda ke bhrashtachar maamalon kii jaanch sheeghra puraa karne ke nirdesh ke alok main satarkta vibhaag kii is karrwai ko dekha ja rahaa he

 nai sarkaar ke sau din puure ho gaye

 janata ko lagata he ki yah sarkaar sahi dhang se kaam kar rahi he

 tufaani chakravaaton kaa namakaran tamaam chetavanee kendron kii ore se kiya jaataa he

 aise main tufaani chakravaaton ke kul 64 naamon kii suchi he

 1955: Wiston Churchill resigns as British Prime Minister

 1979: The country's first Naval Museum opened in Bombay (now Mumbai)
 1993:mashhoor bollywood abhinetri divya bharti kii rahasyamay tareeke se maut ho gai
 1999: The mass killing of 8 lakh 30 thousand pigs was started in Malaysia to protect against the virus named Hendra

 The Janata Dal will not participate in any sit-in demonstration in protest against United Demonetisation
 party ne somvaar ko ' bharat band ' or aakrosh march se bhi alag rahane kaa faisla kiya he
 This decision was taken after the party's core committee meeting held under the chairmanship of Nitish Kumar in Patna on Saturday evening
 party kii bihar ikai ke adhyaksh vashishtha narayan singh ne kaha ki nitish kumaar ne apane faisle kii jaankaree rashtriya janata dal ke adhyaksh lalu yadav or bihar congress adhyaksh ashok choudhary ko bhi de di he
 Nitish argues that the party has previously supported demonetisation and wants to start a campaign against benami property in this campaign against black money
 iske baad dharna pradarshan main bhaag lenaa koi myne nahin rakhata
 Though the party has so far been participating in every program led by the Congress on this issue outside Parliament and beyond, this announcement is also considered a message for former party president Sharad Yadav, who has not only moved away from Nitish Kumar's line in Rajya Sabha Modi government was strongly criticized but also demanded to form a joint parliamentary committee
 nitish sharad yadav ke jantar mantar par mamata banerjee ke dharna par jane se bhi khush nahin the
 It is believed that Sharad Yadav will now separate himself from all programs on this issue
 nitish kaa bihar congress ke adhyaksh ko phone karne kaa yahi arth niklaa ja rahaa he ki congress netaa, khaskar gulam nabi aaazaad or rahul gandhi jo ki is mudde par nitish se jis aakraamak rukh kii ummid kar rahe the vah philhal nitish puraa karne main asamarth hai
 However, Nitish had made it clear at the meeting of the legislature party of the Grand Alliance on Friday that the three parties can take different stand on the national issue
 yah mahagathbandhan bihar ke liye he
 The comments is bich party ne saaf kar diya he ki trinmul adhyaksh, pashchim bengal kii mukhyamantri mamata banerjee ke patna main 30 november ko prastaavit dharne main nitish yaa unki party ke log bhaag nahin lenge
 According to the party's national general secretary KC Tyagi, there is no justification for holding this strike in Patna
 duusari baat rashtriya janata dal se nilambit saansad pappu yadav is dharne main mamata banerjee ke saath baithenge
